 Serif&gt;Financial&#13;instruments of the Group primarily consist of cash and cash equivalents, trade receivables, deposits, prepayments and other receivables,&#13;prepaid land lease, trade payables, receipts in advance, accruals and other payables, and bank borrowings. The carrying values&#13;of the Group&amp;#8217;s financial instruments approximate their fair values, principally because of the short-term maturity of these instruments&#13;or their terms.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;SUMMARY&#13;    OF BUSINESS AND SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING POLICIES&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(a)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Description&#13;    of Business&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Company was incorporated under the laws of the State of Nevada on June 16, 1977. The Company has been in the business of the development&#13;of mineral deposits. During 1983 all activities were abandoned, and the Company had remained inactive until June 29, 2018 when&#13;it acquired the business of Reliant Galaxy International Limited (&amp;#8220;Reliant&amp;#8221;). The Company and its subsidiaries (the&#13;&amp;#8220;Group&amp;#8221;) are principally engaged in the trading of spirits in the People&amp;#8217;s Republic of China (the &amp;#8220;PRC&amp;#8221;).&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Details&#13;of the subsidiaries are set out in note 20 to the consolidated financial statements.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(b)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;The&#13;    basis of consolidation and presentation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Consolidated Financial Statements include the Financial Statements of Oranco, Inc. and the Financial Statements of its wholly-owned&#13;subsidiaries.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Subsidiaries&#13;are all entities over which the Group has control. The Group controls an entity when the Group is exposed to or has rights to&#13;variable returns from its involvement with the investee and has the ability to affect those returns through its power over the&#13;investee. Subsidiaries are fully consolidated from the date on which control is transferred to the Group. They are de-consolidated&#13;from the date that control ceases.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;accompanying financial statements have been prepared in accordance with the U.S. generally accepted accounting principles or GAAP.&#13;The Company operates in one reportable segment and solely within the PRC. Accordingly, no segment or geographic information has&#13;been presented.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Non-controlling&#13;interests are shown as a component of shareholders&amp;#8217; equity on the consolidated balance sheet and the share of the net income&#13;attributable to non-controlling interests is shown as a component of net income in the consolidated statements of operations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Business&#13;Combinations&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;acquisition of other subsidiaries that meet the criteria for business combinations is accounted for using the acquisition method&#13;of accounting. The consideration transferred for the acquisition is the fair values of the assets transferred, the liabilities&#13;incurred to the former owners of the acquiree and the equity interests issued by the Group.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;consideration transferred includes the fair value of any asset or liability resulting from a contingent consideration arrangement.&#13;Identifiable assets acquired and liabilities and contingent liabilities assumed in a business combination are measured initially&#13;at their fair values at the acquisition date. The Group recognizes any non-controlling interest in the acquiree at the non-controlling&#13;interest&amp;#8217;s proportionate share of the recognized amounts of the acquiree&amp;#8217;s identifiable net assets. Acquisition-related&#13;costs are expensed as incurred.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Any&#13;contingent consideration to be transferred by the Group are recognized at fair value at the acquisition date. Subsequent changes&#13;to the fair value of the contingent consideration that is deemed to be an asset or liability is recognized, either in the Statement&#13;of Operations or as a change to other comprehensive income. Contingent consideration that is classified as equity is not remeasured,&#13;and its subsequent settlement is accounted for within equity. Goodwill is initially measured as the excess of the aggregate of&#13;the consideration transferred and the fair value of non-controlling interest over the identifiable net assets acquired and liabilities&#13;assumed.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(c)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Financial&#13;    instruments&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Financial&#13;instruments of the Group primarily consist of cash and cash equivalents, trade receivables, deposits, prepayments and other receivables,&#13;prepaid land lease, trade payables, receipts in advance, accruals and other payables, and bank borrowings. The carrying values&#13;of the Group&amp;#8217;s financial instruments approximate their fair values, principally because of the short-term maturity of these&#13;instruments or their terms.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group has no derivative financial instruments.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(d)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Cash&#13;    and cash equivalents&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Cash&#13;and cash equivalents consist of cash on hand and highly liquid investments which are unrestricted as to withdrawal or use, and&#13;which have maturities of three months or less when purchased.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding: 0; width: 48px; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding: 0; width: 48px; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(e)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Revenue recognition&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group&amp;#8217;s revenues are derived from sales of products recorded net of value added tax (&amp;#8220;VAT&amp;#8221;). Revenue is recognized&#13;when all of the following conditions are met: persuasive evidence of an arrangement exists, delivery of the products has occurred&#13;or services have been rendered, the price is fixed or determinable and collectability is reasonably assured. These criteria are&#13;related to each of the following major revenue generating activities described below.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 70.9pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 35.45pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(i)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Revenue&#13;                                         from the sale of goods is recognized when the significant risks and rewards of ownership&#13;                                         have been transferred to the buyer, provided that the Group maintains neither managerial&#13;                                         involvement to the degree usually associated with ownership nor effective control over&#13;                                         the goods sold. This is usually taken as the time when the goods are delivered and the&#13;                                         customers have accepted the goods.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;                                                                                            &lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 70.9pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 35.45pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(ii)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Interest&#13;                                         income is recognized on an accrual basis using the effective interest method.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(f)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Trade&#13;    receivables and allowance for doubtful accounts&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Trade&#13;receivables are stated at the amount the Group expects to collect. The Group maintains allowances for doubtful accounts for estimated&#13;losses. Management considers the following factors when determining the collectability of specific accounts: historical experience,&#13;creditworthiness of the clients, aging of the receivables and other specific circumstances related to the accounts. Allowance&#13;for doubtful accounts is made and recorded into general and administrative expenses based on the aging of trade receivables and&#13;on any specifically identified receivables that may become uncollectible. Trade receivables which are deemed to be uncollectible&#13;are charged off against the allowance after all means of collection have been exhausted and the potential for recovery is considered&#13;remote. The Company takes a write off of the account balances when the Company can demonstrate all means of collection on the&#13;outstanding balances have been exhausted. There is no allowance for doubtful accounts in these consolidated financial statements.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(g)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Inventories&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Inventories&#13;are stated at the lower of cost or net realizable value. Cost is determined using the weighted average method. The components&#13;of inventories include raw materials, processing cost of finished goods and purchase cost of products. The Group routinely evaluate&#13;the net realizable value of the inventories in light of current market conditions and market trends and record a write-down against&#13;the cost of inventories should the net realizable value falls below the cost.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(h)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Property,&#13;    plant and equipment and depreciation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Property,&#13;plant and equipment are carried at cost less accumulated depreciation and any recorded impairment. Depreciation is calculated&#13;on a straight-line basis over the following estimated useful lives:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; font-weight: bold; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Estimated&#13;    useful life&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 1%; font-weight: bold; padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 29%; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Computer and office&#13;    equipment&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;3 years&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;0-10%&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Repairs&#13;and maintenance are expensed as incurred and asset improvements are capitalized. Consideration is given at each balance sheet&#13;date to determine whether there is any indication of impairment of the carrying amounts of the property, plant and equipment.&#13;The indication could be an unfavorable development of a business or severe economic slowdown as well as reorganization of the&#13;operation. In assessing value in use, the estimated future cash flows are discounted to their present value, based on the time&#13;value of money and the risks specific to the country where the assets are located.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;VAT&#13;    and VAT refund&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;VAT&#13;on sales is charged at 17% on revenue from product sales and is subsequently paid to the PRC tax authorities after netting input&#13;VAT on purchases. The excess of output VAT over input VAT is recognized in other payables, and the excess of input VAT over output&#13;VAT is recognized in other receivables in the consolidated balance sheets.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(j)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Operating&#13;    leases&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Leases&#13;where substantially all the rewards and risks of ownership of assets remain with the lessor are accounted for as operating leases.&#13;Payments made under operating leases are charged to the consolidated statements of operations on a straight-line basis over the&#13;lease periods.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(k)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Foreign&#13;    currency translation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Substantially&#13;all of the Group&amp;#8217;s operations are conducted in China and as a result, the functional and reporting currency of the Group&#13;is the Chinese Renminbi.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Monetary&#13;assets and liabilities denominated in currencies other than the applicable functional currencies are translated into the functional&#13;currencies at the prevailing rates of exchange at the balance sheet date. Transactions in currencies other than the functional&#13;currency are converted into the functional currency at the applicable rates of exchange prevailing at the transaction dates. Transaction&#13;gains and losses are recognized in the consolidated statements of operations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;translating the financial statements of the Company&amp;#8217;s subsidiaries outside the PRC into the reporting currency, assets and&#13;liabilities are translated from the subsidiaries&amp;#8217; functional currencies to the reporting currency at the exchange rate at&#13;the balance sheet date. Equity amounts are translated at historical exchange rates; revenues, expenses, and other gains and losses&#13;are translated using the average rate for the period. Translation adjustments are reported as cumulative translation adjustments&#13;and are shown as a separate component of other comprehensive income/(loss) in the consolidated statements of operations. During&#13;2018 and 2017, such translation adjustments were not material.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(l)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Income&#13;    taxes&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Income&#13;taxes are provided for in accordance with the laws and regulations applicable to the Group as enacted by the relevant tax authorities.&#13;The impact of an uncertain income tax position on the income tax return is recognized at the largest amount that is more-likely-than-not&#13;to be sustained upon audit of the related tax authority. An uncertain income tax position will not be recognized if it has less&#13;than a 50% likelihood of being sustained. Changes in recognition or measurement are reflected in the period in which the change&#13;in judgment occurs. The Group records interest and penalties related to unrecognized tax benefits (if any) in interest expenses&#13;and general and administrative expenses, respectively.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;December 22, 2017, the United States enacted TCJA which instituted fundamental changes to the taxation of multinational corporations,&#13;including a reduction the U.S. corporate income tax rate to 21% beginning in 2018. The TCJA also requires a one-time transition&#13;tax on the mandatory deemed repatriation of the cumulative earnings of the Company&amp;#8217;s foreign subsidiary as of December 31,&#13;2017. To determine the amount of this transition tax, the Company must determine the amount of earnings generated since inception&#13;by the relevant foreign subsidiary, as well as the amount of non-U.S. income taxes paid on such earnings, in addition to potentially&#13;other factors. The Company acquired the foreign operations on 29 June 2018, hence the Company does not have any qualifying earnings&#13;or profits from its foreign subsidiary under the transition tax calculation thus no transition tax is payable.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(m)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Fair&#13;    value measurement&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group defines fair value as the price that would be received from selling an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly&#13;transaction between market participants at the measurement date.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;When&#13;determining the fair value measurements for assets and liabilities required or permitted to be recorded at fair value, the Group&#13;considers the principal or most advantageous market in which it would transact and it considers assumptions that market participants&#13;would use when pricing the asset or liability.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group&amp;#8217;s financial instruments include cash and cash equivalents, term deposits, trade and other receivables, and trade and&#13;other payables. The Group considers the carrying amounts approximate fair value because of the short maturity of these financial&#13;instruments.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(n)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Business&#13;    combinations&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;a business combination achieved in stages, the Group remeasures its previously held equity interest in the acquire immediately&#13;before obtaining control at its acquisition-date fair value and the re-measurement gain or loss, if any, is recognized in earnings.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(o)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Transactions&#13;    between entities under common control&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;When&#13;accounting for a transfer of assets or exchange of shares between entities under common control of the Group, the carrying amounts&#13;of the assets and liabilities transferred shall remain unchanged subsequent to the transaction, and no gain or loss shall be recorded&#13;in the Group&amp;#8217;s consolidated statements of operations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(p)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Commitments&#13;    and contingencies&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;the normal course of business, the Group is subject to loss contingencies, such as legal proceedings and claims arising out of&#13;its business, that cover a wide range of matters, including, among others, government investigations, shareholder lawsuits, and&#13;non-income tax matters. An accrual for a loss contingency is recognized when it is probable that a liability has been incurred&#13;and the amount of loss can be reasonably estimated. If a potential material loss contingency is not probable but is reasonably&#13;possible, or is probable but cannot be estimated, then the nature of the contingent liability, together with an estimate of the&#13;range of possible loss if determinable and material, is disclosed.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(q)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Recently&#13;    issued accounting pronouncements not yet adopted&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;January 2017, the FASB issued ASU No. 2017-01, &amp;#8220;Business Combinations: Clarifying the Definition of a Business&amp;#8221; (&amp;#8220;ASU&#13;2017-01&amp;#8221;). ASU 2017-01 clarifies the definition of a business for determining whether transactions should be accounted for&#13;as acquisitions (or disposals) of assets or businesses. ASU 2017-01 is effective for annual periods and interim periods within&#13;those annual periods beginning after December 15, 2017, and early adoption is permitted. The Company will adopt this standard&#13;on July 1, 2018 and will apply the standard to any future business combinations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;August 2016, FASB issued ASU No. 2016-15, Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments. The standard provides new&#13;authoritative guidance addressing eight specific cash flow issues with the objective of reducing the existing diversity in practice&#13;in how certain transactions are presented and classified in the statement of cash flows. The standard is effective for the Group&#13;in the first quarter of the fiscal year 2019. The Company does not expect the adoption of this standard to have a significant&#13;impact on its consolidated financial statements.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;February 2016, FASB issued ASU No. 2016-02, Leases. The standard increases transparency and comparability among organizations&#13;by requiring companies to recognize leased assets and related liabilities on the balance sheet and disclose key information about&#13;leasing arrangements. This standard is effective for the Group in the first quarter of the fiscal year 2020. The Group is evaluating&#13;the impact the adoption of this standard will have on its consolidated financial statements.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;May 2014, FASB issued ASU, 2014-09, Revenue from Contracts with Customers. The standard is a comprehensive new revenue recognition&#13;model that requires revenue to be recognized in a manner to depict the transfer of goods or services to a customer at an amount&#13;that reflects the consideration expected to be received in exchange for those goods or services. In August 2015, FASB issued ASU&#13;2015-14, Revenue from Contracts with Customers, to defer the effective date of ASU 2014-09 by one year to annual reporting periods&#13;beginning after December 15, 2017, but permits entities to adopt the original effective date if they choose. Based on the Group&amp;#8217;s&#13;preliminary assessment, it does not expect the adoption of the standard to result in material changes in revenue. Further, deferred&#13;costs to obtain contracts, which will be recognized in sales and marketing expense in future periods, are not expected to be material.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;adoption of the standard in the consolidated financial statements for the financial year ended June 30, 2019 will have no significant&#13;impact to the provision for income taxes and will have no impact to the net cash used in, or generated by, operating, investing,&#13;or financing activities in the Group&amp;#8217;s consolidated statements of cash flows.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;td style=padding: 0; width: 48px; text-indent: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding: 0; width: 48px; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(e)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Revenue recognition&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group&amp;#8217;s revenues are derived from sales of products recorded net of value added tax (&amp;#8220;VAT&amp;#8221;). Revenue is recognized&#13;when all of the following conditions are met: persuasive evidence of an arrangement exists, delivery of the products has occurred&#13;or services have been rendered, the price is fixed or determinable and collectability is reasonably assured. These criteria are&#13;related to each of the following major revenue generating activities described below.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 70.9pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 35.45pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(i)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Revenue&#13;                                         from the sale of goods is recognized when the significant risks and rewards of ownership&#13;                                         have been transferred to the buyer, provided that the Group maintains neither managerial&#13;                                         involvement to the degree usually associated with ownership nor effective control over&#13;                                         the goods sold. This is usually taken as the time when the goods are delivered and the&#13;                                         customers have accepted the goods.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;                                                                                            &lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Property, plant&#13;    and equipment and depreciation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Property,&#13;plant and equipment are carried at cost less accumulated depreciation and any recorded impairment. Depreciation is calculated&#13;on a straight-line basis over the following estimated useful lives:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1in; background-color: White&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; font-weight: bold; text-align: justify&gt;Category&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 1%; font-weight: bold; padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 30%; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid&gt;Estimated useful life&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 1%; font-weight: bold; padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 29%; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid&gt;Estimated residual values&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: rgb(204

255)&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=background-color: White&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;Building&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: center&gt;20 years&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: center&gt;0-10%&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=background-color: White&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;Computer and office equipment&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: center&gt;3 years&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: center&gt;0-10%&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;(k)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Foreign currency&#13;    translation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Substantially&#13;all of the Group&amp;#8217;s operations are conducted in China and as a result, the functional and reporting currency of the Group&#13;is the Chinese Renminbi.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Monetary&#13;assets and liabilities denominated in currencies other than the applicable functional currencies are translated into the functional&#13;currencies at the prevailing rates of exchange at the balance sheet date. Transactions in currencies other than the functional&#13;currency are converted into the functional currency at the applicable rates of exchange prevailing at the transaction dates. Transaction&#13;gains and losses are recognized in the consolidated statements of operations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(l)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Income taxes&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;Income taxes are provided&#13;for in accordance with the laws and regulations applicable to the Group as enacted by the relevant tax authorities. The impact&#13;of an uncertain income tax position on the income tax return is recognized at the largest amount that is more-likely-than-not&#13;to be sustained upon audit of the related tax authority. An uncertain income tax position will not be recognized if it has less&#13;than a 50% likelihood of being sustained. Changes in recognition or measurement are reflected in the period in which the change&#13;in judgment occurs. The Group records interest and penalties related to unrecognized tax benefits (if any) in interest expenses&#13;and general and administrative expenses, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(m)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Fair value measurement&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;Group defines fair value as the price that would be received from selling an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly&#13;transaction between market participants at the measurement date.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;When&#13;determining the fair value measurements for assets and liabilities required or permitted to be recorded at fair value, the Group&#13;considers the principal or most advantageous market in which it would transact and it considers assumptions that market participants&#13;would use when pricing the asset or liability.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(q)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Recently issued&#13;    accounting pronouncements not yet adopted&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;January 2017, the FASB issued ASU No. 2017-01, &amp;#8220;Business Combinations: Clarifying the Definition of a Business&amp;#8221; (&amp;#8220;ASU&#13;2017-01&amp;#8221;). ASU 2017-01 clarifies the definition of a business for determining whether transactions should be accounted for&#13;as acquisitions (or disposals) of assets or businesses. ASU 2017-01 is effective for annual periods and interim periods within&#13;those annual periods beginning after December 15, 2017, and early adoption is permitted. The Company will adopt this standard&#13;on July 1, 2018 and will apply the standard to any future business combinations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;In August 2016, FASB issued ASU&#13;No. 2016-15, Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments. The standard provides new authoritative guidance addressing&#13;eight specific cash flow issues with the objective of reducing the existing diversity in practice in how certain transactions are&#13;presented and classified in the statement of cash flows. The standard is effective for the Group in the first quarter of the fiscal&#13;year 2019. The Company does not expect the adoption of this standard to have a significant impact on its consolidated financial&#13;statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;In February 2016, FASB issued&#13;ASU No. 2016-02, Leases. The standard increases transparency and comparability among organizations by requiring companies to recognize&#13;leased assets and related liabilities on the balance sheet and disclose key information about leasing arrangements. This standard&#13;is effective for the Group in the first quarter of the fiscal year 2020. The Group is evaluating the impact the adoption of this&#13;standard will have on its consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;May 2014, FASB issued ASU, 2014-09, Revenue from Contracts with Customers. The standard is a comprehensive new revenue recognition&#13;model that requires revenue to be recognized in a manner to depict the transfer of goods or services to a customer at an amount&#13;that reflects the consideration expected to be received in exchange for those goods or services. In August 2015, FASB issued ASU&#13;2015-14, Revenue from Contracts with Customers, to defer the effective date of ASU 2014-09 by one year to annual reporting periods&#13;beginning after December 15, 2017, but permits entities to adopt the original effective date if they choose. Based on the Group&amp;#8217;s&#13;preliminary assessment, it does not expect the adoption of the standard to result in material changes in revenue. Further, deferred&#13;costs to obtain contracts, which will be recognized in sales and marketing expense in future periods, are not expected to be material.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The&#13;adoption of the standard in the consolidated financial statements for the financial year ended June 30, 2019 will have no significant&#13;impact to the provision for income taxes and will have no impact to the net cash used in, or generated by, operating, investing,&#13;or financing activities in the Group&amp;#8217;s consolidated statements of cash flows.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company is subject to taxes&#13;in the USA. The Company has had no taxable income under Federal or State tax laws.  Serif&gt;CONTRIBUTION PLAN IN THE PRC&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;As stipulated by the PRC state&#13;regulations, the subsidiaries in the PRC participate in the state-run defined contribution retirement scheme. All employees are&#13;entitled to an annual pension payment equal to a fixed proportion of the average basic salary of the geographical area of their&#13;last employment at their retirement date. The PRC subsidiaries are required to make contributions to the local social security&#13;bureau at 29.4% to 37.4% of the previous year&amp;#8217;s average basic salary amount of the geographical area where the employees&#13;are under employment with the PRC subsidiaries. The Group has no obligation for the payment of pension benefits beyond the annual&#13;contributions as set out above.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif&gt;21.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman
