 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;REVERSE MERGER&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;June 29, 2018, Oranco, Inc. acquired 100% of the issued capital of Reliant in a share for share exchange with the shareholders&#13;of Reliant at that time. Due to the relative size of the companies, the shareholders of Reliant became the majority shareholders&#13;in the consolidated group.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Pursuant&#13;to the share for share exchange, Oranco shall issue an aggregated 349,296,000 new shares of common stock, with par value of $0.001&#13;per share, of which 28,000,000 were issued at the closing date of June 29, 2018, and the remaining 321,296,000 shares shall be&#13;issued at the completion of the increase of the Company&amp;#8217;s authorized shares. The 321,296,000 shares are classified as fully&#13;paid-up shares to be issued as of June 30, 2018.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;td style=width: 48px; font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px; text-align: justify; font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;(b)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;The basis of consolidation and presentation&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Consolidated Financial Statements&#13;include the Financial Statements of Oranco, Inc. and the Financial Statements of its wholly-owned subsidiaries.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;Subsidiaries are all entities over&#13;which the Group has control. The Group controls an entity when the Group is exposed to or has rights to variable returns from its&#13;involvement with the investee and has the ability to affect those returns through its power over the investee. Subsidiaries are&#13;fully consolidated from the date on which control is transferred to the Group. They are de-consolidated from the date that control&#13;ceases.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;The accompanying financial statements&#13;have been prepared in accordance with the U.S. generally accepted accounting principles or GAAP. The Company operates in one reportable&#13;segment and solely within the PRC. Accordingly, no segment or geographic information has been presented.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Non-controlling&#13;interests are shown as a component of shareholders&amp;#8217; equity on the consolidated balance sheet and the share of the net income&#13;attributable to non-controlling interests is shown as a component of net income in the consolidated statements of operations.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Business&#13;Combinations&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;The acquisition of other subsidiaries&#13;that meet the criteria for business combinations is accounted for using the acquisition method of accounting. The consideration&#13;transferred for the acquisition is the fair values of the assets transferred, the liabilities incurred to the former owners of&#13;the acquiree and the equity interests issued by the Group.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;The consideration transferred includes&#13;the fair value of any asset or liability resulting from a contingent consideration arrangement. Identifiable assets acquired and&#13;liabilities and contingent liabilities assumed in a business combination are measured initially at their fair values at the acquisition&#13;date. The Group recognizes any non-controlling interest in the acquiree at the non-controlling interest&amp;#8217;s proportionate share&#13;of the recognized amounts of the acquiree&amp;#8217;s identifiable net assets. Acquisition-related costs are expensed as incurred.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; padding: 0; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Prepaid&#13;land lease, net, consists of the following:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

var Show = {};
Show.LastAR = null
Show.hideAR = function(){
	Show.LastAR.style.display = 'none';
};
Show.showAR = function ( link
 id
 win ){
	if( Show.LastAR ){
		Show.hideAR();
	}
	var ref = link;
	do {
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	} while (ref && ref.nodeName != 'TABLE');
	if (!ref || ref.nodeName != 'TABLE') {
		var tmp = win ?
			win.document.getElementById(id) :
			document.getElementById(id);
		if( tmp ){
			ref = tmp.cloneNode(true);
			ref.id = '';
			link.parentNode.appendChild(ref);
		}
	}
	if( ref ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		Show.LastAR = ref;
	}
};
Show.toggleNext = function( link ){
	var ref = link;
	do{
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	}while( ref.nodeName != 'DIV' );
	if( ref.style &&
		ref.style.display &&
		ref.style.display == 'none' ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}
	}else{
		ref.style.display = 'none';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}
	}
};
